dark:bg-slate-1200 ><tr class= border-b border-border ><th class= h-10 px-4 text-left text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wide >Problem</th><th class= h-10 px-4 text-left >Fix</th></tr></thead><tbody class= &amp;_tr:last-child :border-0 ><tr class= border-b border-border ><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-foreground align-top whitespace-nowrap >State mismatch error</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >state in the callback doesn&#x27;t match stored value</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >Store state in sessionStorage before redirecting, and don&#x27;t regenerate it on page load</td></tr><tr class= border-b border-border ><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-foreground align-top whitespace-nowrap >invalid_grant on token exchange</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >code_verifier doesn&#x27;t match the challenge, or code expired/already used</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >Send the original code_verifier, not a newly generated one; exchange the code immediately</td></tr><tr class= border-b border-border ><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-foreground align-top whitespace-nowrap >Redirect URI mismatch</td><td 120px >Check for trailing slashes, http vs https, port numbers</td></tr><tr class= border-b border-border ><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-foreground align-top whitespace-nowrap >invalid_client</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >Wrong client_id</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >Verify your credentials from the Deriv dashboard</td></tr><tr class= border-b border-border ><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-foreground align-top whitespace-nowrap >Login form shows instead of signup</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >Missing prompt=registration</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >Add class= my-4 ><div class= w-full overflow-x-auto rounded-xl border border-border scrollbar-thin scrollbar-thumb-border scrollbar-track-transparent ><table class= w-full min-w- 600px caption-bottom text-sm border-collapse ><thead class= &amp;_tr :border-b &amp;_tr :border-border bg-slate-1200/10 dark:bg-slate-1200 ><tr class= border-b border-border ><th class= h-10 px-4 text-left text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wide >Problem</th><th class= h-10 px-4 text-left text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wide >Likely cause</th><th class= h-10 px-4 text-left text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wide >Fix</th></tr></thead><tbody class= &amp;_tr:last-child :border-0 ><tr class= border-b border-border ><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-foreground align-top whitespace-nowrap >State mismatch error</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >state in the callback doesn&#x27;t match stored value</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >Store state in sessionStorage before redirecting, and don&#x27;t regenerate it on page load</td></tr><tr class= border-b border-border ><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-foreground align-top whitespace-nowrap >invalid_grant on token exchange</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >code_verifier doesn&#x27;t match the challenge, or code expired/already used</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >Send the original code_verifier, not a newly generated one; exchange the code immediately</td></tr><tr class= border-b border-border ><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-foreground align-top whitespace-nowrap >Redirect URI mismatch</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >URL doesn&#x27;t exactly match what&#x27;s registered</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >Check for trailing slashes, http vs https, port numbers</td></tr><tr class= border-b border-border ><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-foreground align-top whitespace-nowrap >invalid_client</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >Wrong client_id</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >Verify your credentials from the Deriv dashboard</td></tr><tr class= border-b border-border ><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-foreground align-top whitespace-nowrap >Login form shows instead of signup</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >Missing prompt=registration</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >Add prompt=registration to the authorization URL</td></tr><tr class= border-b border-border ><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-foreground align-top whitespace-nowrap >Signup not tracked to partner</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >Missing or wrong UTM parameters</td><td class= px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground align-top min-w- 120px >Verify your tracking token parameter (one of t, affiliate_token, sidi, or ca) matches the one shown in your referral link, and that utm_source, utm_medium, and utm_campaign are all present and correct</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div><h2 class= text-xl font-semibold text-foreground mt-10 mb-4 scroll-mt-24 id=
